it be a town of red brick or of brick that would have be red if the smoke and ash have allow it but as matter stand it be a town of unnatural red and black like the paint face of a savage
it be a town of machinery and tall chimney out of which interminable serpent of smoke trail themselves for ever and ever and never get uncoil
it have a black canal in it and a river that run purple with ill-smell dye and vast pile of build full of window where there be a rattle and a trembling all day long and where the piston of the steam-engine work monotonously up and down like the head of an elephant in a state of melancholy madness
it contain several large street all very like one another and many small street still more like one another inhabit by people equally like one another who all go in and out at the same hour with the same sound upon the same pavement to do the same work and to whom every day be the same as yesterday and to-morrow and every year the counterpart of the last and the next
these attribute of coketown be in the main inseparable from the work by which it be sustain against they be to be set off comfort of life which find their way all over the world and elegancie of life which make we will not ask how much of the fine lady who could scarcely bear to hear the place mention

chapter vi the starlight the sunday be a bright sunday in autumn clear and cool when early in the morning sissy and rachael meet to walk in the country
as coketown cast ash not only on its own head but on the neighbourhood s too after the manner of those pious person who do penance for their own sin by put other people into sackcloth it be customary for those who now and then thirst for a draught of pure air which be not absolutely the most wicked among the vanity of life to get a few mile away by the railroad and then begin their walk or their lounge in the field

in the distance one way coketown show as a black mist in another distance hill begin to rise in a third there be a faint change in the light of the horizon where it shine upon the far-off sea
